Order of the segments in a URL.\\n556: # Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\\n557: # Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\\n558: # of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\\n559: _URL_SEGMENTS = [\\n560:     (\\n561:         'host',\\n562:         lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n563:         lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n564:     (\\n565:         'port',\\n566:         lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\\n567:         lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\\n568:     (\\n569:         'path',\\n570:         lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n571:         lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n572:     (\\n573:         'query',\\n574:         lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n575:         lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n576:     (\\n577:         'anchor',\\n578:         lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n579:         lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n580: ]\\n581: \\n582: \\n583: def incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\\n584:     \\\"\\\"\\\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\\n585: \\n586:     Args:\\n587:         url: The current url\\n588:         incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\\n589:         count: The number to increment or decrement by\\n590:         segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\\n591:                   'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\\n592:                   Default: {'path', 'query'}\\n593: \\n594:     Return:\\n595:         The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\\n596: \\n597:     Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\\n598:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n599:     if not url.isValid():\\n600:         raise InvalidUrlError(url)\\n601: \\n602:     if segments is None:\\n603:         segments = {'path', 'query'}\\n604:     valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\\n605:     if segments - valid_segments:\\n606:         extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\\n607:         raise IncDecError(\\\"Invalid segments: {}\\\".format(\\n608:             ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\\n609: \\n610:     # of information. Let me understand the bugs more clearly by analyzing what the task says and what the code actually does:\n\nLooking at the _URL_SEGMENTS definition (lines 559-580):\n```python\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n```\n\nThe issue is that `PrettyDecoded` mode decodes percent-encoded characters. So if we have `%3A` (colon), it becomes `:` when we call `getter(url)`.\n\nThen the regex on line 618:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\\\d+)(.*)',\n                     getter(url))\n```\n\nThis regex tries to find numbers NOT preceded by `%` or `%.`, but since the string is already decoded, the `%` is gone! So if we have `%35` (which is the digit 5), it gets decoded to `5`, and then the regex might pick up that `5` as a valid number to increment. The core problem is that decoding the URL segments strips away the percent-encoding markers, so the regex's negative lookbehind assertions can't properly identify which numbers were originally encoded and should be left alone.\n\nWhen a URL like `http://localhost/%3A5` gets decoded to `:5`, the function finds and increments the `5` to `6`, resulting in `:6` instead of the intended `%3A6`. The encoded sequence gets corrupted because the decoding happens before the number matching logic runs. Additionally, the regex's attempt to exclude percent-encoded digits using `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` becomes ineffective once those percent signs are removed from the string.\n\nTo verify this behavior, I should construct test cases that expose these issues—particularly one with an encoded colon followed by a number like `%3A5`, and another checking whether the function properly handles negative values despite the safeguards in place. that the negative lookbehind assumes the string hasn't been decoded yet. When the string is already decoded, the `%` character won't be there, so the lookbehind check becomes meaningless. I need to reconsider whether the regex is even being applied to the right string at the right time. Let me trace through what happens with a concrete example like `http://localhost/%3A5` - after decoding it becomes `http://localhost/:5`, and at that point the regex should match the final digit and increment it correctly, but the lookbehind for `%` is no longer relevant since the percent encoding is already gone.\n\nThe real issue seems to be that percent-encoded sequences containing digits get corrupted. Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted (e.g., %3A5 becomes %3A6 but corrupts %3A)\n2. Negative values are allowed when they should error\n3. URL-encoded data (like %20 for space) is lost or incorrectly handled\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n# Add qutebrowser to path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom qutebrowser.utils import urlutils\n\n\nclass TestIncdecEncodedSequences:\n    \"\"\"Test increment/decrement with percent-encoded sequences.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_in_sequence_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %35 (encoded 5) in URL is not treated as a number to increment.\n\n        The sequence %35 encodes the digit 5, but it should not be modified\n        when looking for numbers to increment. We want to increment a different\n        number if one exists.\n\n        Bug: The current implementation may incorrectly match the 3 or 5 in %35\n        and increment it, corrupting the percent-encoded sequence.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %35 is the encoding for the character '5' (ASCII 53 = 0x35)\n        # This URL has %35 followed by the literal number 5\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%355\")\n\n        # Increment should only touch the trailing 5, not the %35\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%356\")\n\n        # The bug: the result might be different because %35 gets decoded and\n        # the 3 or 5 within it gets incremented\n        assert result.path() == expected.path(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.path()}, got {result.path()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_number_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with %3A (encoded colon) followed by a number.\n\n        %3A is the percent-encoding for ':' (colon). When we have %3A5,\n        only the 5 should be incremented, not the 3 in %3A.\n\n        Bug: The implementation may incorrectly interpret the 3 in %3A as\n        a number to increment.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A5\")\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A6\")\n\n        assert result.toString() == expected.toString(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        assert \"%3A\" in result.toString(), \\\n            f\"Encoded sequence %3A was corrupted: {result.toString()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_space_with_number_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with %20 (encoded space) followed by a number.\n\n        %20 encodes a space character. This should be preserved, and only\n        a trailing number (if present) should be incremented.\n\n        Bug: The %20 may get decoded to a literal space, which could corrupt\n        the URL structure.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/hello%20world5\")\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/hello%20world6\")\n\n        assert result.toString() == expected.toString(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        # Verify the encoded sequence is intact\n        assert \"%3A\" in result.toString(), \\\n            f\"Encoded sequence %3A was corrupted: {result.toString()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_anchor_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment with encoded sequence in anchor/fragment.\n\n        Bug: Anchors with percent-encoded sequences followed by numbers\n        may get corrupted.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/#%3A5\")\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'anchor'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/#%3A6\")\n\n        assert result.fragment() == expected.fragment(), \\\n            f\"Expected fragment {expected.fragment()}, got {result.fragment()}\"\n        # Verify the encoded sequence is intact\n        assert \"%3A\" in result.toString(), \\\n            f\"Encoded sequence %3A was corrupted: {result.toString()}\"\n\n\nclass TestIncdecNegativeValues:\n    \"\"\"Test that decrement operations properly reject negative results.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_decrement_one_by_two(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 1 by 2 raises an error, not negative value.\n\n        Bug: The implementation may allow decrements that produce negative\n        numbers, e.g., decrementing /page_1 by 2 produces /page_-1 instead\n        of raising an error.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_1\")\n\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError) as exc_info:\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n\n        assert \"decrement\" in str(exc_info.value).lower(), \\\n            f\"Error message should mention decrement: {exc_info.value}\"\n\n    def test_decrement_zero_by_one(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 0 by 1 raises an error.\n\n        Bug: The implementation may allow zero to become negative.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_0\")\n\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError):\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_decrement_small_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing a small number by a large count raises error.\n\n        Bug: Decrementing /v5 by 10 may produce /v-5 instead of erroring.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/v5\")\n\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError):\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=10, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_decrement_large_by_exact_amount(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing exactly to zero is allowed.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_5\")\n\n        # Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted (e.g., %3A5 becomes %3A6 but corrupts %3A)\n2. Negative values are allowed when they should error\n3. URL-encoded data (like %20 for space) is lost or incorrectly handled\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n# Add qutebrowser to path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom qutebrowser.utils import urlutils\n\n\nclass TestIncdecEncodedSequences:\n    \"\"\"Test increment/decrement with percent-encoded sequences.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_in_sequence_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %35 (encoded 5) in URL is not treated as a number to increment.\n\n        The sequence %35 encodes the digit 5, but it should not be modified\n        when looking for numbers to increment. We want to increment a different\n        number if one exists.\n\n        Bug: The current implementation may incorrectly match the 3 or 5 in %35\n        and increment it, corrupting the percent-encoded sequence.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %35 is the encoding for the character '5' (ASCII 53 = 0x35)\n        # This URL has %35 followed by the literal number 5\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%355\")\n\n        # Increment should only touch the trailing 5, not the %35\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%356\")\n\n        # The bug: the result might be different because %35 gets decoded and\n        # the 3 or 5 within it gets incremented\n        assert result.path() == expected.path(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.path()}, got {result.path()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_number_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with %3A (encoded colon) followed by a number.\n\n        %3A is the percent-encoding for ':' (colon). When we have %3A5,\n        only the 5 should be incremented, not the 3 in %3A.\n\n        Bug: The implementation may incorrectly interpret the 3 in %3A as\n        a number to increment.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A5\")\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A6\")\n\n        assert result.toString() == expected.toString(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        assert \"%3A\" in result.toString(), \\\n            f\"Encoded sequence %3A was corrupted: {result.toString()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_space_with_number_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with %20 (encoded space) followed by a number.\n\n        %20 encodes a space character. This should be preserved, and only\n        a trailing number (if present) should be incremented.\n\n        Bug: The %20 may get decoded to a literal space, which could corrupt\n        the URL structure.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/hello%20world5\")\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/hello%20world6\")\n\n        assert result.toString() == expected.toString(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        # Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise urlutils.InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string not preceded by regex '%' or '%.'\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\nclass TestIncdecEncodedSequences:\n    \"\"\"Test increment/decrement with percent-encoded sequences.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_in_sequence_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %35 (encoded 5) in URL is not treated as a number to increment.\n\n        The sequence %35 encodes the digit 5, but it should not be modified\n        when looking for numbers to increment. We want to increment a different\n        number if one exists.\n\n        Bug: The current implementation may incorrectly match the 3 or 5 in %35\n        and increment it, corrupting the percent-encoded sequence.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %35 is the encoding for the character '5' (ASCII 53 = 0x35)\n        # This URL has %35 followed by the literal number 5\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%355\")\n\n        # Increment should only touch the trailing 5, not the %35\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%356\")\n\n        # The bug: the result might be different because %35 gets decoded and\n        # the 3 or 5 within it gets incremented\n        assert result.path() == expected.path(), \\\n            f\"Expected {expected.path()}, got {result.path()}\"\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_number_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with %3A (encoded colon) followed by a number.\n\n        %3A is the percent-encoding for ':' (colon).
